bar à®à®²à¯à®²à®¤à¯ bhar à®à®©à¯à®©à¯à®®à¯ à®à®°à®¿à®¯ à®µà¯à®°à¯à®à¯à®à¯à®²à¯ à®ªà®±à¯à®±à®¿ For instance. the root bar or bhar particularly if we minde the words derived from Latin ferre and adopted English such as, for instance, fertile, far (barley), farina, barley-flower, reference, deference, conference, difference, inference, preference, transference and all the rust, would more than a hundred English words.
